# 配置交换功能 - 宝塔已部署站点一键覆盖更新
# 用法：复制本文件全部内容，粘贴到宝塔终端执行。
# 说明：只覆盖程序文件，不覆盖 data 用户数据；会自动备份旧文件。
set -e
APP="$(systemctl show toolbox-admin -p WorkingDirectory --value 2>/dev/null || true)"
if [ -z "$APP" ] || [ "$APP" = "/" ]; then APP="/www/wwwroot/gjx.vst76.cn"; fi
if [ ! -d "$APP" ]; then echo "站点目录不存在：$APP"; exit 1; fi
cd "$APP"

TOOLBOX_UPDATE_B64
base64 -d "$B64" > "$PKG"
rm -rf "$TMP"
mkdir -p "$TMP"
tar -xzf "$PKG" -C "$TMP"
python3 -m py_compile "$TMP/app.py"
mkdir -p "backup-config-exchange-update-$TS"
[ -f app.py ] && cp -a app.py "backup-config-exchange-update-$TS/app.py"
[ -d wwwroot ] && cp -a wwwroot "backup-config-exchange-update-$TS/wwwroot"
[ -d client-template ] && cp -a client-template "backup-config-exchange-update-$TS/client-template"
install -m 0644 "$TMP/app.py" app.py
mkdir -p wwwroot client-template
install -m 0644 "$TMP/wwwroot/index.html" wwwroot/index.html
install -m 0644 "$TMP/wwwroot/admin.js" wwwroot/admin.js
install -m 0644 "$TMP/wwwroot/styles.css" wwwroot/styles.css
install -m 0644 "$TMP/client-template/ToolboxClient.cs" client-template/ToolboxClient.cs
install -m 0644 "$TMP/client-template/toolbox.hta" client-template/toolbox.hta
install -m 0644 "$TMP/client-template/launch.cmd" client-template/launch.cmd
rm -rf data/client-cache data/client-jobs
systemctl restart toolbox-admin
sleep 2
systemctl is-active --quiet toolbox-admin
curl -fsS http://127.0.0.1:5088/api/public/brand >/dev/null
printf '\n同步完成。备份目录：%s\n' "$APP/backup-config-exchange-update-$TS"
printf '请刷新后台页面，然后进入：配置交换。\n'
